#
# Collect metadata on the sysroot and perform sanity checks.
#
mkdir -p "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi"
#
# Collect symbol information.
#
"llvm-nm" --defined-only "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi"/libc.a "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi"/libwasi-emulated-*.a "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi"/*.o \
    |grep ' [[:upper:]] ' |sed 's/.* [[:upper:]] //' |LC_ALL=C sort > "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/defined-symbols.txt"
for undef_sym in $("llvm-nm" --undefined-only "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi"/libc.a "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi"/libc-*.a "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi"/*.o |grep ' U ' |sed 's/.* U //' |LC_ALL=C sort |uniq); do \
    grep -q '\<'$undef_sym'\>' "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/defined-symbols.txt" || echo $undef_sym; \
done | grep -v "^__mul" > "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/undefined-symbols.txt"
grep '^_*imported_wasi_' "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/undefined-symbols.txt" \
    > "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi/libc.imports"
#
# Generate a test file that includes all public C header files.
#
cd "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/include" && \
  for header in $(find . -type f -not -name mman.h -not -name signal.h -not -name times.h -not -name resource.h |grep -v /bits/ |grep -v /c++/); do \
      echo '#include <'$header'>' | sed 's/\.\///' ; \
done |LC_ALL=C sort >/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/include-all.c ; \
cd - >/dev/null
#
# Test that it compiles.
#
clang -O2 -DNDEBUG --target=wasm32-wasi -fno-trapping-math -Wall -Wextra -Werror -Wno-null-pointer-arithmetic -Wno-unused-parameter -Wno-sign-compare -Wno-unused-variable -Wno-unused-function -Wno-ignored-attributes -Wno-missing-braces -Wno-ignored-pragmas -Wno-unused-but-set-variable -Wno-unknown-warning-option -mthread-model single -isystem "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/include" -fsyntax-only "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/include-all.c" -Wno-\#warnings
#
# Collect all the predefined macros, except for compiler version macros
# which we don't need to track here.
#
clang -O2 -DNDEBUG --target=wasm32-wasi -fno-trapping-math -Wall -Wextra -Werror -Wno-null-pointer-arithmetic -Wno-unused-parameter -Wno-sign-compare -Wno-unused-variable -Wno-unused-function -Wno-ignored-attributes -Wno-missing-braces -Wno-ignored-pragmas -Wno-unused-but-set-variable -Wno-unknown-warning-option -mthread-model single -isystem "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/include" "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/include-all.c" \
    -isystem /home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/include \
    -std=gnu17 \
    -E -dM -Wno-\#warnings \
    -D_ALL_SOURCE \
    -U__llvm__ \
    -U__clang__ \
    -U__clang_major__ \
    -U__clang_minor__ \
    -U__clang_patchlevel__ \
    -U__clang_version__ \
    -U__clang_literal_encoding__ \
    -U__clang_wide_literal_encoding__ \
    -U__GNUC__ \
    -U__GNUC_MINOR__ \
    -U__GNUC_PATCHLEVEL__ \
    -U__VERSION__ \
    -U__FLOAT128__ \
    -U__NO_MATH_ERRNO__ \
    -U__BITINT_MAXWIDTH__ \
    -U__FLT_EVAL_METHOD__ -Wno-builtin-macro-redefined \
    | sed -e 's/__[[:upper:][:digit:]]*_ATOMIC_\([[:upper:][:digit:]_]*\)_LOCK_FREE/__compiler_ATOMIC_\1_LOCK_FREE/' \
    | grep -v '^#define __FLT16_' \
    | grep -v '^#define __\(BOOL\|INT_\(LEAST\|FAST\)\(8\|16\|32\|64\)\|INT\|LONG\|LLONG\|SHRT\)_WIDTH__' \
    > "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi/predefined-macros.txt"
# Check that the computed metadata matches the expected metadata.
# This ignores whitespace because on Windows the output has CRLF line endings.
diff -wur "/home/theos/wasi-libc/expected/wasm32-wasi" "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share/wasm32-wasi"
#
# Create empty placeholder libraries.
#
for name in m rt pthread crypt util xnet resolv dl; do \
    llvm-ar crs "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib/wasm32-wasi/lib${name}.a"; \
done
#
# The build succeeded! The generated sysroot is in /home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot.
#
mkdir -p "/tmp/wasi-libc"
cp -r "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/lib" "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/share" "/home/theos/wasi-libc/sysroot/include" "/tmp/wasi-libc"
